msg:First of all, I would like to praise Xiaoyue at the front desk for her attentive service, friendly attitude and high professional quality.
I have stayed in Shangri-La in many cities and I approve of it. The following are just some shortcomings, I hope it will be improved and I will come again next time:
1. The pressure of the shower in the bathroom is too high (even if the faucet is turned down, there is not much improvement). The water sprayed out feels like a needle prick for adults. Be careful with children and try it again.
2. The handle of the drawer is really sharp. My child and I were scratched by the tip when we walked by it. I think this should not be an accident. My child is already 10 years old and is a big child. Parents who bring babies to stay must be careful to take care of their children and stay away from similar sharp places.
3. The TV is still an analog signal, and the clarity is really worrying.
4·I vaguely remember that the first time I stayed in Shangri-La was in Hangzhou in 2005. Many years have passed. The toothbrushes of Shangri-La hotels in many cities are still those with very hard and thick bristles. It is recommended to improve them and replace them with fine-bristled toothbrushes with good elasticity and softness.
Come on, I love Shangri-La very much, so I hope you will become better!
